<script type="text/javascript">
  var xitiForm = "";
  $(function(){
    

          $(".prodRefLoc").live("click", function(e){
        if(!lm.tools.getCookie("contextRefLocales")) {
          e.preventDefault();
          lm.contextualisation.openPopin();
          setTimeout(function(){
            $('#overlay').remove();
            $("#overlay_obligatoire").css("opacity","0.8").show();
            $('#layer_context').addClass('layer_obligatoire')
          },200);
          $("#urlRedirect").val($(this).attr("href"));
        }
      });
    
    $("#CtxRdrct").val((window.location.pathname+window.location.search).replace(/&/g,'%26').replace(/\+/g,'%2B'));
  })
</script>
